Dan has really come a really far way, in spite of how much growth he has had for over a decade, from Diamond Minecart mod reviews in early MC beta stages to modern time games. It's really awesome to see the childhood Youtuber of millions of people continue to grow as time goes on. I have been a fan since Dan hit 500,000 followers yes when I was younger I watched him without knowing who he was but later in time looking back at those videos he posted and I aimlessly watched gave me the feeling of my entire childhood. Dan is one of the nicest and funniest creators I've known and Its sad how time passes so fast It's already been almost 10 years since he hit 1M subs one thing I really enjoyed, or a matter of fact, doing, was when he posted mod reviews but after I finished watching the video I went on Minecraft and tried to do the mod myself and couldn't do it so I eventually give up and go back to watching more of your videos. I was amazed how you can make Dr. T (best villager ever) quote and quote, TALK, of course I know all the behind the scenes by now but when I was younger, different story lol. Can't forget Grim, OFC! Yeah, later I actually know how to do these mods that he did but they in present time are now old and outdated so its a shame that very few mods actually can function correctly from 1.7.10 and above. My favorite mod showcase was the roller coaster one where a clown asked Dan to build a roller coaster, (obviously it was part of the main scripted events in the mod showcase) but it was really enjoying just watching him build the roller coaster and me having a good laugh over it. My dad always used to say "why watch the person play the game when you can actually play the game for yourself?" Yes I totally understand but watching DanTDM was a different experience when it comes to watching people play the game when you can actually play the game. I also remember buying a hoodie merch many years ago and I was searching through my drawer and found the hoodie and many childhood memories flooded back into my brain.
